main(){
    while(1):
        executeShell(int timeout)
} ^LNDW1PGC

getCommandFromInput() {
    pointer = malloc()
    read()
    trimWhiteSpaces()
    return pointer
} ^oy3BR6v6

executeShell(int timeout) {
    char* command;
    command = getCommandFromInput()
} ^E2zzeUv2
